<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> (479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частый.html>ча́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">částyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">částo</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ча́сто" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:чаща.html>ча́ще</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>frequently, often</li>
<li>close, thickly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дере́вья</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посаженный.html>поса́жены</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">derévʹja posáženy <b>částo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the trees are planted close together</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***частокол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:частокол.html>частоко́л</a> (13207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частый.html>ча́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">částyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kol</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Other sources suggest it's from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">częstokół</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">palisade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the same meaning.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частокол.html>частоко́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">častokól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частокол.html>частоко́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частокол.html>частоко́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частокол.html>частоко́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>palisade, paling, fence</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:частый.html>ча́стый</a> (731)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čęstъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частый.html>ча́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">částyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:чаща.html>ча́ще</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>frequent</li>
<li>thick, thickset, dense, close</li>
<li>quick, rapid</li></ol>

***часть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a> (209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">častĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čęstь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">častʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>part
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больший.html>бо́льшей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́стью</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bólʹšej <b>částʹju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mostly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больший.html>бо́льшей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сти</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po bólʹšej <b>části</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">for the most part</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>share</li>
<li>piece
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́м</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>častjám</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in pieces</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>department, section</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unit <i>(regimental or smaller sized and administratively self-contained)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> line, branch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> police station</li></ol>

***чахнувший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чахнуть.html>ча́хнувший</a> (25866)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахнуть.html>ча́хнувший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čáxnuvšij</span>)
</p>

***чахнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чахнуть.html>ча́хнуть</a> (25866)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахнуть.html>ча́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čáxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачахнуть.html>зача́хнуть</a></b>)

***чахотка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чахотка.html>чахо́тка</a> (19639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахнуть.html>ча́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čáxnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахнуть.html>ча́х</a>(нуть)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ота́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-otá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахотка.html>чахо́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čaxótka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахотка.html>чахо́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахотка.html>чахо́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чахотка.html>чахо́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>consumption, phthisis <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">atrophy of the body as a result of tuberculosis</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***чача.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чача.html>ча́ча</a> (17144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Georgian language">Georgian</a></span> <i class="Geor mention" lang="ka">ჭაჭა</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ka-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">č̣ač̣a</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чача.html>ча́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čáča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чача.html>ча́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чача.html>ча́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чача.html>ча́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chacha - traditionally a clear strong liquor, which is sometimes called "vine vodka," "grape vodka," or "Georgian vodka."
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1988</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrei_Gromyko" class="extiw" title="w:Andrei Gromyko">Andrei Gromyko</a>,  <cite>Memoirs</cite>, Moscow, page 196—205:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> я́лте, <a href = vnd.unilang:например.html>наприме́р</a>, ста́лин похваливал <a href = vnd.unilang:грузинский.html>грузи́нские</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сухой.html>сухи́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вина</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потом.html>потом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́л</a>:<br />—А <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грузинский.html>грузи́нскую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:виноградный.html>виногра́дную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дку</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чача.html>ча́чу</a></b>?</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V Jálte, naprimér, Stálin poxvalival gruzínskije suxíje vina, a potom sprosíl:<br />—A vy znájete gruzínskuju vinográdnuju vódku — <b>čáču</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In Yalta, for example, Stalin praised Georgian dry wines, and then he asked:<br />— Do you know, by any chance, the Georgian grape vodka — <b>chacha</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаша.html>ча́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čáša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаша.html>ча́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čaša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čaša</i>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаять.html>ча́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-яние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-janije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаяние.html>ча́яние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čájanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаяние.html>ча́яния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаяние.html>ча́яния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаяние.html>ча́яний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>expectation, hope, dream, aspiration
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паче.html>па́че</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:сверх.html>сверх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чаяние.html>ча́яния</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">páče / sverx <b>čájanija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">beyond expectation, contrary to expectation, unexpectedly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чаянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чаять.html>ча́янный</a> (16895)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаять.html>ча́янный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čájannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаять.html>ча́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čàjati</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чванливый.html>чванли́вый</a> (30389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чва́нить(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čvánitʹ(sja)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to swagger, to be conceited</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чванливый.html>чванли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čvanlívyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>snobby, arrogant <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having excessive pride</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>stuffy</li>
<li>peacocky</li>
<li>snot-nosed</li></ol>

***чей.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чей</a> (799)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьjь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čej</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>interrogative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>Чей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Čej</b> étot dom?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Whose</b> house is this?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>Чья</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Čʹja</b> éta kníga?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Whose</b> book is this?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>Чьи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Čʹi</b> éti dénʹgi?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Whose</b> money is this?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>Чьё</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Čʹjó</b> éto palʹtó?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Whose</b> overcoat is this?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чьё</a></b>? <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чьё</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto <b>čʹjó</b>? Ja znáju, <b>čʹjó</b> éto.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Whose</b> is this? I know <b>whose</b> it is.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>Чью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взя́ли</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Čʹju</b> knígu vy vzjáli?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Whose</b> book did you take?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чьей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́гой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S <b>čʹjej</b> bumágoj on idjót?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Whose</b> paper is he going with?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:студент.html>студе́нта</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>нашли́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Studénta, <b>čʹju</b> knígu vy našlí, ješčó net dóma.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The student <b>whose</b> book you found is not home yet.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> anyone's
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1879</b>,  Николай Семёнович <a href = vnd.unilang:лесок.html>Леско́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikolai_Leskov" class="extiw" title="w:Nikolai Leskov">Nikolai Semyonovich Leskov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:предисловие.html>Предисло́вие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цикл.html>ци́клу</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:праведник.html>Пра́ведники</a>»</cite>  | <cite>Preface to the "Righteous Men" series</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:неужто.html>неу́жто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мое́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чьей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сской</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видать.html>вида́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:кроме.html>кро́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дря́ни</a>?</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak, — dúmal ja, — neúžto v sámom déle ni v mojéj, ni v jevó i ni v <b>čʹjej</b> inój rússkoj dušé ne vidátʹ ničevó, króme drjáni?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What, I thought, can it really be that neither in mine nor in his, nor in <b>anyone</b> else'<b>s</b> Russian soul is there to be seen anything but rubbish?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1968</b>,  Александр Исаевич Солженицын (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleksandr_Solzhenitsyn" class="extiw" title="w:Aleksandr Solzhenitsyn">Aleksandr Isayevich Solzhenitsyn</a>),  chapter 6, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> кругле <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвом</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/In_the_First_Circle" class="extiw" title="w:In the First Circle">In the First Circle</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заниматься.html>занима́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подобный.html>подо́бной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>них</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>Во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́ком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чае</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чьи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>труды́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Niktó, kážetsja, ne zanimálsja podóbnoj rabótoj do nix. Vo vsjákom slúčaje, oní ne napáli ni na <b>čʹi</b> trudý.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">No one, it seems, had undertaken a similar project before them. In any case, they did not come across <b>any researchers'</b> works (on the subject).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***чеканить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чеканить.html>чека́нить</a> (22037)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чека́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čekán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканить.html>чека́нить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čekánitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отчеканить.html>отчека́нить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mint, to coin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканить.html>чека́нить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:монета.html>моне́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čekánitʹ</b> monétu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mint coins; coin money</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stamp (an image on metal)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканить.html>чека́нить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:медаль.html>меда́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čekánitʹ</b> medáli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike/stamp medals</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to perform repetitive actions forcefully and with separation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканить.html>чека́нить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čekánitʹ</b> slová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rap out the words</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканить.html>чека́нить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čekánitʹ</b> šag</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to measure out one's pace</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chase, to caulk</li></ol>

***чеканка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>чеканка</a> (32045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканить.html>чека́нить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čekánitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>чека́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čekánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканка.html>чека́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканка.html>чека́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканка.html>чека́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>minting, coining</li>
<li>stamping <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an image on metal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>performing actions forcefully and with separation</li>
<li>enunciating with force</li>
<li>beating a tread</li>
<li>relief image in metal</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чека́н</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čekán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чеканный.html>чека́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čekánnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***чекист.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чекист.html>чеки́ст</a> (5607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чека.html>чека́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Čeká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ист</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ist</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чекист.html>чеки́ст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čekíst</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чекист.html>чеки́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чекист.html>чеки́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чекист.html>чеки́стов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чеки́стка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Chekist</i>; an agent of the Cheka, the Soviet Russian secret police from 1917 to 1922, replacing the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Okhrana" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Okhrana">Okhrana</a> secret police of Tsarist Russia; succeeded by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joint_State_Political_Directorate" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joint State Political Directorate">OGPU</a> and NKVD</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> KGB man, FSB agent; a national security official employed by any of the state security intelligence agencies of the Soviet Union or Russian Federation</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:челнок.html>челно́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čelnók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:челнок.html>челнока́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:челнок.html>челноки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:челнок.html>челноко́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">челно́чный</b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čelo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kelh₃os</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чело.html>чело́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čeló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чело.html>чела́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чело.html>че́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:честь.html>чел</a></b>)
</p>

***человек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> (34)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьlověkъ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čelověkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čelovék</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ки</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>люде́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></strong><sup>*</sup></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ков</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Nominative plural - rare, poetic, other cases of <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></span></b> in plural are used with numbers.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>person, human being, man
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1866</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Фёдор достое́вский</span> (Fyodor Dostoyevsky),  chapter 4, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9F%D1%80%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D1%83%D0%BF%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B5_%D0%B8_%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BA%D0%B0%D0%B7%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B5_(%D0%94%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B5%D0%B2%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9)/%D0%A7%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C_I/%D0%93%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B0_IVRussian" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Преступление и наказание (Достоевский)/Часть I/Глава IV"><a href = vnd.unilang:преступление.html>Преступле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ние</a></a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Prestuplenije i nakazanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></cite>  | <cite>Crime and Punishment</cite> | , part 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">отгово́рка-то <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>кака́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:капитальный.html>капита́льная</a>: „уж <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:дескать.html>де́скать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:деловой.html>делово́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b> Пётр петро́вич, <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деловой.html>делово́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> жени́ться-то <a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почтовый.html>почто́вых</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:железный.html>желез́ной</a> доро́ге“.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otgovórka-to kakája kapitálʹnaja: „už takój, déskatʹ, delovój <b>čelovék</b> Pjótr Petróvič, takój delovój <b>čelovék</b>, što i ženítʹsja-to ináče ne móžet, kak na počtóvyx, čutʹ ne na želeźnoj doróge“.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A magnificent excuse: "Pyotr Petrovitch is such a busy <b>man</b> that even his wedding has to be done post-haste, almost by express."</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>(<i>collective, no plural</i>) human race</li>
<li><i>also plural when used with cardinal words</i>:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">odín <b>čelovék</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one person</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dva <b>čelovéka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">two persons, people</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹ <b>čelovék</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">five persons, people</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">désjatʹ <b>čelovék</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten persons, people</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvádcatʹ <b>čelovék</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">twenty persons, people</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvádcatʹ odín <b>čelovék</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">twenty-one persons, people</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvádcatʹ dva <b>čelovéka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">twenty-two persons, people</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Usage of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b> with numerals: The genitive plural form <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b> is used only after whole numbers (tens, hundreds, thousands, millions, etc.), numbers ending in <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> and after <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néskolʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skólʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also - <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>люде́й</a></b>), and sometimes after <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mnógo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Use genitive singular of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b> after simple or compound numbers ending in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (2), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (3), or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četýre</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (4). Use nominative singular of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b>  after simple or compound numbers ending in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1). Otherwise plural of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b> is a form <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></b>.</li>
<li>The derivations, e.g. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">получелове́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polučelovék</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and compound words with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></b>, e.g. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снежный.html>сне́жный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">snéžnyj čelovék</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разумный.html>разу́мный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čelovék razúmnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, do not necessarily follow the same usage.</li></ul>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:представитель.html>представи́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:млекопитающее.html>млекопита́ющих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a> <i>Homo</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:отряд.html>отря́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:примат.html>прима́тов</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:узкий.html>у́зком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смысл.html>смы́сле</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <i>Homo sapiens</i> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***человечек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:человечек.html>челове́чек</a> (4810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čelovék</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ек</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ek</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человечек.html>челове́чек</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čelovéček</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человечек.html>челове́чка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человечек.html>челове́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человечек.html>челове́чков</a></b>)
</p>
